profeſſor chirurgerie verie learned painfull gentleman told montanus written morbus pilaris called pilaris affectio ſoone little child taken diſeaſe crie take extreamely yet one perceiue cauſe ſhould ſo brings oftentimes euen graue diſeaſe drawes along epylepticall convulſions becauſe sinewes come foorth backebone ſcattred ſide ouer burthened filld ſome fuliginous vapour haires bred great length continuitie carried directlie braine whither come cauſe diſeaſe woman countrie languedocke becauſe common diſeaſe make great reckoning doe helpe manner palme hand rub bottome child backe raines downe crupper bone ſo long till feele pore skin top verie ſtiffe pricking haires come foorth like vnto hogg briſtles ſoone ſee come foorth pull away nayles elſe ſuch little pincer woman vſe pull haire
